\u2500\u2500 DB \u2500\u2500\nlet db;\nfunction openDB() {\n  return new Promise((res,rej) => {\n    const r = indexedDB.open('stageset3', 1);\n    r.onupgradeneeded = e => {\n      const d = e.target.result;\n      ['songs','setlists','notes'].forEach(s => { if (!d.objectStoreNames.contains(s)) d.createObjectStore(s,{keyPath:'id'}); });\n    };\n    r.onsuccess = e => { db = e.target.result; res(); };\n    r.onerror = rej;\n  });\n}\nconst txs = (s,m='readonly') => db.transaction(s,m).objectStore(s);\nconst dbGet = (s,k) => new Promise((r,j) => { const q=txs(s).get(k); q.onsuccess=()=>r(q.result); q.onerror=j; });\nconst dbAll = s => new Promise((r,j) => { const q=txs(s).getAll(); q.onsuccess=()=>r(q.result); q.onerror=j; });\nconst dbPut = (s,v) => new Promise((r,j) => { const q=txs(s,'readwrite').put(v); q.onsuccess=()=>r(); q.onerror=j; });\nconst dbDel = (s,k) => new Promise((r,j) => { const q=txs(s,'readwrite').delete(k); q.onsuccess=()=>r(); q.onerror=j; });\nconst uid = () => crypto.randomUUID ? crypto.randomUUID() : Date.now().toString(36)+Math.random().toString(36).slice(2);\n\n// \u2500\u2500 SYNC \u2500\u2500\nconst SYNC_KEY = 'stageset_shared_v3';\nlet online = navigator.onLine;\nlet bc; try { bc = new BroadcastChannel('stageset3'); } catch(e) {}\nwindow.addEventListener('online', () => { online=true; updateSyncUI(); syncIn(); });\nwindow.addEventListener('offline', () => { online=false; updateSyncUI(); });\nfunction updateSyncUI() {\n  const cls = 'sync-pip'+(online?'':' offline');\n  document.getElementById('syncPip').className = cls;\n  const sp = document.getElementById('syncPipSidebar');\n  if (sp) sp.className = cls;\n  const sl = document.getElementById('syncLabelSidebar');\n  if (sl) sl.textContent = online ? 'Online' : 'Local only';\n}\nasync function syncOut() {\n  if (!online) return;\n  const [songs,sets] = await Promise.all([dbAll('songs'),dbAll('setlists')]);\n  const b = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(SYNC_KEY)||'{\"s\":{},\"l\":{}}');\n  songs.forEach(x=>b.s[x.id]=x); sets.forEach(x=>b.l[x.id]=x); b.ts=Date.now();\n  localStorage.setItem(SYNC_KEY,JSON.stringify(b));\n  if(bc) bc.postMessage({type:'u',b});\n}\nasync function syncIn() {\n  try {\n    const b = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(SYNC_KEY)||'{}');\n    if(b.s) for(const x of Object.values(b.s)) await dbPut('songs',x);\n    if(b.l) for(const x of Object.values(b.l)) await dbPut('setlists',x);\n    renderAll();\n  } catch(e) {}\n}\nif(bc) bc.onmessage = async e => {\n  if(e.data?.type==='u') {\n    const b=e.data.b;\n    if(b.s) for(const x of Object.values(b.s)) await dbPut('songs',x);\n    if(b.l) for(const x of Object.values(b.l)) await dbPut('setlists',x);\n    renderAll(); showToast('Synced','ok');\n  }\n};\n\n// \u2500\u2500 STATE \u2500\u2500\nlet currentUser = '';\nlet currentSetId = null;\nlet currentSetSongs = [];\nlet noteTab = 'default';\nlet editingNote = false;\nlet dragIdx = null;\nlet editingSets = false;\nconst pageStack = [];\n\n// \u2500\u2500 NAVIGATION \u2500\u2500\nfunction showPage(id) {\n  document.querySelectorAll('.page').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('active','behind'));\n  if (pageStack.length) document.getElementById(pageStack[pageStack.length-1]).classList.add('behind');\n  pageStack.push(id);\n  document.getElementById(id).classList.add('active');\n}\nfunction goBack() {\n  if (pageStack.length <= 1) return;\n  stopScroll();\n  if (bpmTimer) { clearInterval(bpmTimer); bpmTimer=null; }\n  const leaving = pageStack.pop();\n  const lp = document.getElementById(leaving);\n  lp.style.transition = 'transform 0.3s cubic-bezier(0.4,0,0.2,1)';\n  lp.style.transform = 'translateX(100%)';\n  setTimeout(() => { lp.style.transform=''; lp.classList.remove('active','behind'); }, 320);\n  const ret = pageStack[pageStack.length-1];\n  document.getElementById(ret).classList.remove('behind');\n  document.getElementById(ret).classList.add('active');\n}\nfunction navTo(tab) {\n  document.querySelectorAll('.nav-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));\n  const nb = document.getElementById('nav-'+tab);        <button class=\"note-tab ${noteTab==='default'?'active':''}\" onclick=\"switchNoteTab('default',${idx})\">Default Notes</button>\n          <button class=\"note-tab ${noteTab==='mine'?'active':''}\" onclick=\"switchNoteTab('mine',${idx})\">My Notes</button>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"scroll-toolbar\" id=\"scrollToolbar\" style=\"margin-left:12px;\">\n          <button class=\"scroll-play-btn\" id=\"scrollPlayBtn\" onclick=\"toggleScroll()\" title=\"Auto-scroll\">\n            ${scrollPlaying\n              ? `<svg viewBox=\"0 0 24 24\" ${buildNoteContent(activeNote, idx)}\n    </div>`;\n\n  setupSwipe(idx);\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500 BPM METRONOME \u2500\u2500\nfunction startBpmFlash(bpm) {\n  if (bpmTimer) { clearInterval(bpmTimer); bpmTimer=null; const c=document.getElementById('bpmChip'); if(c) c.classList.remove('flash'); return; }\n  const interval = 60000 / bpm;\n  const chip = document.getElementById('bpmChip');\n  if (!chip) return;\n  let on = false;\n  function flash() { on=!on; chip.classList.toggle('flash', on); }\n  flash();\n  bpmTimer = setInterval(flash, interval / 2);\n  setTimeout(() => { if(bpmTimer){clearInterval(bpmTimer);bpmTimer=null;} const c=document.getElementById('bpmChip'); if(c) c.classList.remove('flash'); }, interval * 16 + 200);\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500 AUTO SCROLL \u2500\u2500\nfunction toggleScroll() {\n  scrollPlaying ? stopScroll() : startScroll();\n}\nfunction startScroll() {\n  if (scrollPlaying) return;\n  scrollPlaying = true;\n  updateScrollUI();\n  let last = null;\n  let accumulated = 0;\n  function step(ts) {\n    if (!scrollPlaying) return;\n    if (last !== null) {\n      const pxPerSec = scrollSpeed * 5;\n      accumulated += (pxPerSec * (ts - last)) / 1000;\n      if (accumulated >= 1) {\n        const area = document.getElementById('noteArea');\n        if (!area) { stopScroll(); return; }\n        const move = Math.floor(accumulated);\n        accumulated -= move;\n        area.scrollTop += move;\n        if (area.scrollTop + area.clientHeight >= area.scrollHeight - 2) {\n          stopScroll(); return;\n        }\n      }\n    }\n    last = ts;\n    scrollTimer = requestAnimationFrame(step);\n  }\n  scrollTimer = requestAnimationFrame(step);\n}\nfunction stopScroll() {\n  scrollPlaying = false;\n  if (scrollTimer) { cancelAnimationFrame(scrollTimer); scrollTimer = null; }\n  updateScrollUI();\n}\nfunction updateScrollUI() {\n  const btn = document.getElementById('scrollPlayBtn');\n  if (!btn) return;\n  btn.innerHTML = scrollPlaying\n    ? `<svg viewBox=\"0 0 24 24\" fill=\"currentColor\"><rect x=\"6\" y=\"5\" width=\"4\" height=\"14\" rx=\"1\"/><rect x=\"14\" y=\"5\" width=\"4\" height=\"14\" rx=\"1\"/></svg>`\n    : `<svg viewBox=\"0 0 24 24\" fill=\"currentColor\"><path d=\"M8 5v14l11-7z\"/></svg>`;\n}\nfunction changeSpeed(delta) {\n  scrollSpeed = Math.max(1, Math.min(10, scrollSpeed + delta));\n  const s = currentSetSongs[currentSongIdx];\n  if (s) songScrollSpeeds[s.id] = scrollSpeed;\n  const label = document.getElementById('scrollSpeedLabel');\n  if (label) label.textContent = `\u00d7${scrollSpeed}`;\n}\n\nfunction buildNoteContent(text, idx) {\n  if (editingNote) {\n    return `<textarea class=\"note-edit-area\" id=\"noteEditArea\" placeholder=\"Add notes\u2026\">${esc(text)}</textarea>\n    <button class=\"save-btn\" onclick=\"saveCurrentNote(${idx})\">Save Notes</button>`;\n  }\n  return `<div class=\"note-display${text?'':' empty'}\">${text?esc(text):'No notes yet.'}</div>\n  <button class=\"edit-note-btn\" onclick=\"startEditNote(${idx})\">\n    <svg viewBox=\"0 0 24 24\" fill=\"none\" stroke=\"currentColor\" stroke-width=\"1.8\" style=\"width:15px;height:15px\"><path d=\"M11 4H4a2 2 0 00-2 2v14a2 2 0 002 2h14a2 2 0 002-2v-7\"/><path d=\"M18.5 2.5a2.121 2.121 0 013 3L12 15l-4 1 1-4 9.5-9.5z\"/></svg>\n    ${text?'Edit notes':'Add notes'}\n  </button>`;\n}\n\nasync function switchNoteTab(tab, idx) { noteTab=tab; editingNote=false; await renderSongPage(idx); }\nfunction startEditNote(idx) { {\n    await dbPut('notes',{id:`${currentUser||'me'}_${s.id}`,text,updatedAt:Date.now()});\n  }\n  editingNote=false; await renderSongPage(idx); showToast('Saved','ok');\n}\nfunction swipeTo(idx) {\n  if (idx<0||idx>=currentSetSongs.length) return;\n  stopScroll();\n  if (bpmTimer) { clearInterval(bpmTimer); bpmTimer=null; }\n  editingNote=false; renderSongPage(idx);\n}\nfunction setupSwipe(idx) {\n  const body = document.getElementById('songPageBody');\n  let sx=0, sy=0;\n  const ts = e => { sx=e.touches[0].clientX; sy=e.touches[0].clientY; };\n  const te = e => {\n    const dx=e.changedTouches[0].clientX-sx, dy=e.changedTouches[0].clientY-sy;\n    if (Math.abs(dx)<50||Math.abs(dy)>Math.abs(dx)) return;\n    if (dx<0&&idx<currentSetSongs.length-1) swipeTo(idx+1);\n    else if (dx>0&&idx>0) swipeTo(idx-1);\n  };\n  if (body._ts) { body.removeEventListener('touchstart',body._ts); body.removeEventListener('touchend',body._te); }\n  body._ts=ts; body._te=te;\n  body.addEventListener('touchstart',ts,{passive:true});\n  body.addEventListener('touchend',te,{passive:true});\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500 PICKER \u2500\u2500\nfunction openPicker() { document.getElementById('pickerSearch').value=''; document.getElementById('pickerModal').classList.remove('hidden'); renderPicker(); }\nfunction closePicker() { function renderPicker() {\n  const set=await dbGet('setlists',currentSetId);\n  const songIdsInSet = (set?.songs||[]).map(s=>typeof s==='string'?s:s?.songId).filter(Boolean);\n  let songs=await songs.sort((a,b)=>a.title.localeCompare(b.title));\n  const el=document.getElementById('pickerList');\n  if(!songs.length){el.innerHTML='<div r.onupgradeneeded = e => {\\n      const d = e.target.result;\\n      ['songs','setlists','notes'].forEach(s => { if (!d.objectStoreNames.contains(s)) d.createObjectStore(s,{keyPath:'id'}); });\\n    };\\n    r.onsuccess = e => { db = e.target.result; res(); };\\n    r.onerror = rej;\\n  });\\n}\\nconst txs = (s,m='readonly') => db.transaction(s,m).objectStore(s);\\nconst dbGet = (s,k) => new \\u2500\\u2500 SYNC \\u2500\\u2500\\nconst SYNC_KEY = 'stageset_shared_v3';\\nlet online = navigator.onLine;\\nlet bc; try { bc = new BroadcastChannel('stageset3'); } catch(e)
